The Reaction to Qingdao's Increased Land Tax

Citizens Send Representatives to Petition for Exemption

The Municipal Government Agrees to Consider Postponing the Implementation

Qingdao Dispatch: The Qingdao Municipal Government's Finance Bureau recently sent a letter to the General Chamber of Commerce, requesting the nomination of two members for the Private Land Evaluation Committee, which is scheduled to be formally established by the end of this month, in order to re-determine the land tax rate and increase revenue. The General Chamber of Commerce convened meetings of various members and landowners twice, but without any results. At 2:00 PM on the 22nd, the third meeting was held at the General Chamber of Commerce, with over a thousand attendees. Ding Jingchen, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, presided over the meeting. Everyone agreed that in this time of economic recession, the current private land tax rate is already high, and they cannot afford to bear any additional burden. The public finds it difficult to accept the issue of electing members to organize the evaluation committee. Even the rental rights for government-owned land are harmful to the people and should be abolished. It was agreed to send representatives to petition the authorities to completely eliminate the plan. The entire assembly unanimously passed the motion and elected forty representatives, including Ye Chunchi, to go to the municipal government to petition at 2:00 PM on the 23rd. The municipal government held a temporary meeting that was delayed until 3:30 PM. Secretary-General Hu Jiafeng, Finance Bureau Director Guo Binghe, and Xiong Shubin, the third section chief of the Finance Bureau, received the representatives. After the representatives stated their intentions, they said that they had already paid rent for the land. The additional rental rights fee is like buying land, and it is difficult to bear the burden of paying for both new leases and renewals. The current tax rate for private land is 6%. According to the Finance Bureau's regulations, the best land is 38 yuan per square foot, which is several times higher than the original price, which is too high. Therefore, they asked for consideration of the situation and for the cancellation of the plan. Secretary-General Hu and the representatives had a thorough discussion. He said that the rental rights fee has been in place for a long time and no problems have occurred. If it is canceled, it will only increase disputes. This issue should be discussed at length after the mayor returns to Qingdao. The re-evaluation of private land can be postponed temporarily. It will be implemented after the national land law is promulgated. The representatives, seeing that the petition had achieved results, took their leave and departed. (December 24th)

The Jinan Telephone Company Appeal Case Opens (Continued)

Next, the agent of the respondent, Yoshida, expressed his views, which were translated by Ugaji Takao. He stated briefly that he requested the dismissal of the appeal and that the appellant bear the appeal costs. The appellant claimed: (1) The director had no authority to sign the contract; (2) Ma Guanhe colluded with Dongtuo. These points will be debated in eight sections. First, the general manager is the director of the legal entity, and the director has the authority to represent the legal entity. Article 27 of the General Principles of the Civil Code, which your country has promulgated, has this provision. Ma Guanhe, the principal debtor in this case, is both a director and the general manager, which is not disputed by both parties. According to Article 13 of the telephone company's articles of association, the general manager has the power to execute all matters. Also, according to Article 158 of the Company Law, the director can represent the company. With these various provisions, the general manager has the authority to borrow 440,000 yuan. The director's seal has legal effect. Second, the appellant argues that Article 199 of the Company Law stipulates that company bonds cannot be raised without a resolution of a special board meeting. However, Articles 190 to 198 all relate to the regulations of company bonds. The case involves common debt, not company bonds, so it cannot be restricted. Third, the appellant argues that Ma Guanhe had no authority to borrow money. However, Ma is the general manager and director. According to the company's articles of association, there are no restrictions on the director's authority. Therefore, even though this case involves a joint guarantee, he still has the authority. Furthermore, this debt is for operating capital, and the directors are all aware of it. Therefore, there are no shortcomings in Dongtuo's case. The appellant also argues that Ma Guanhe's actions were improper and detrimental to the telephone company. This is an internal matter. The appellant can request Ma to compensate, but it cannot restrict this case. Therefore, the original judgment, which stated that if Ma Guanhe, as the general manager and director, has harmed the company, it cannot be transferred to a third party, is very accurate. Fourth, the appellant argues that this loan was not introduced by a third party and that Ma Guanhe and Dongtuo handled it secretly. It was not filed with the Chinese authorities, but only with the Japanese consulate, which means that Dongtuo was unwilling to file it. This is worthless because the presence or absence of a third party has no impact on the loan. Whether it is filed with the authorities or not also has no relationship to the loan. Moreover, there was indeed an introducer at the time, and the reason it was not filed with the national authorities was that your country did not have a registration law at the time, so it was only filed with the Japanese consulate. Therefore, this case is by no means secret. Fifth, the appellant argues that the loan is outside the scope of business. However, this loan is for expanding the telephone company's business, which is clearly within the scope of business. Dongtuo trusted the telephone company's articles of association, so it made this loan. The appellant is naturally responsible. If Ma Guanhe borrowed the money with malicious intent, the telephone company should directly hold Ma Guanhe accountable, and it should not involve a third party. Sixth, the appellant argues that the disposition of all collateral in the contract violates laws and regulations. However, according to the principle of freedom to enter into contracts, it can be established as long as it does not violate good morals and public order. All the collateral was approved by the directors. Because of the large amount of 440,000 yuan, Dongtuo had to require collateral. At that time, your country did not have an auction law, so the contract could only state free auction. As for giving priority to employing Japanese people and the loan matters, both parties agreed at the time, and it has nothing to do with the debt. Seventh, the appellant argues that Article 9 of Regulation 135 of the Ministry of Transportation regarding privately established telephones stipulates that if a private telephone is auctioned, both parties must report to the Ministry of Transportation, otherwise it is invalid. The appellant claims that the respondent and Ma Guanhe privately entered into the agreement without reporting it to the Ministry of Transportation, so it is not valid. This article refers to the regulations for sales contracts and does not apply to this case. Eighth, in summary, can the appellant prove that Ma Guanhe was not a director and general manager at the time of the loan? Is there proof that the respondent colluded with Ma Guanhe? The respondent recognized that Ma had the authority to represent the company. The contract he signed with a third party is valid. Therefore, the appellant must be fully responsible for this debt. The appellant's appeal is completely unreasonable. The presiding judge asked, "In the first volume, there is a handwritten letter from Ma Guanhe stating that the loan has nothing to do with the telephone company. What year was it?" Yan Chenghan replied, "It was the sixteenth year, when Ma was the director of the Zhili Finance Bureau. An Shanzhi questioned him about this." (The judge took the letter for Yoshida to read.) Yoshida said, "It is not known whether this letter was written after Ma and the telephone company reconciled. Even if it is true, it was written under duress." The judge asked, "Is the term five years?" Yoshida said, "It is fifteen years. After the term expired, there were several negotiations at the Foreign Affairs Office." Yan Chenghan replied, "The telephone company is unaware." Yoshida then presented Ma's handwritten letter, a business card from the telephone company's general affairs, and an insurance policy. Yan Chenghan replied, "The evidence is insufficient. Even if it is true, it cannot obligate the telephone company to repay the debt." At this point, the testimony was read, signed, and the court was adjourned. (December 20th)

Shaanxi Welcomes Yu Youren

And Welcomes the Entire Provincial Party Committee

Xi'an Dispatch: Yu Youren arrived in Xi'an yesterday (the 18th). Yang Hucheng and others welcomed him outside Zhongshan Gate and set up his residence in Zhang Xiangchu's house in Juhuayuan. Today (the 19th), various circles held a grand welcome meeting for President Yu at the New City Drill Ground. Because the entire Provincial Party Committee had also arrived in Shaanxi, they also welcomed the entire Provincial Party Committee members at the same time. All agencies, organizations, schools, and troops participated. The meeting opened at 12:00 noon. Nan Ruji delivered the opening address, stating briefly that they had originally planned to hold three separate welcome meetings for President Yu, the Party Committee, and the Provincial Committee. However, because time is precious, they are welcoming President Yu and the entire Provincial Party Committee members at the same time today. Next, Yang Hucheng delivered a welcome speech, stating briefly that Shaanxi was able to break through Tongguan in the shortest possible time and end the war. On the surface, it was due to the efforts of the armed comrades who entered Shaanxi. However, the reason why this result could be achieved was due to the revolutionary seeds sown by President Yu in Shaanxi and the revolutionary talents cultivated. In the future, they still hope that President Yu will guide everything so that they have something to follow. Now that the Party Provincial Committee has arrived in Shaanxi, a new Shaanxi can be realized in the future. Next, Ma Qingwan delivered a welcome speech, describing the three periods of Yu's revolution in Shaanxi. Next, Zhao Yuru, the president of Zhongda, delivered a welcome speech, hoping that Yu and the Provincial Party Committee would work hard to build a truly new Shaanxi. Kang Jiyao then delivered a welcome speech on behalf of the people, stating briefly that any undertaking should be carried out with compassion. Next, Yu delivered a reply, stating briefly that he did not dare to accept the welcome. He is a Shaanxi commoner with a beard. He leads all the people of Shaanxi in welcoming the Provincial Party Committee members who are attending the meeting today. Shaanxi has been barren and drought-stricken as never before. According to foreign investigations, approximately two million famine victims have died. At present, there are starving people everywhere. Fortunately, Director He (Yingqin) proposed at the Fourth Plenary Session to allocate 8 million yuan in relief loans to Shaanxi. My request is only a share of the majority and not the power of me alone, so please do not spread false rumors. I also have two proposals: (1) All employees serving in Shaanxi should wear black gauze on a certain day to commemorate the disaster and hope that such a great disaster will never happen again. (2) Pray to the spirit of the Premier in Heaven and all the gods of Heaven and Earth, so that all the Shaanxi children who have escaped the disaster, been sold to the outside of the pass, and are wandering can have good circumstances. I have returned to Shaanxi several times, but the results have always been tears. The great disaster in Shaanxi means that I cannot evade my fault. Fortunately, the revolutionary army and the revolutionary comrades have now arrived in Shaanxi. This time, I may be able to leave the pass and return to Beijing with a smile. Next, Yu Guozhen of the Party Committee gave a reply, discussing the disasters, banditry, suffering of the people in Shaanxi, and the crimes of Feng in Shaanxi, in a very thorough manner. Next, Li Fanyi of the Provincial Committee gave a speech, stating briefly that he believes that the committee members who have come to Shaanxi this time will never exploit the people of Shaanxi. Next, Hu Yimin of the Provincial Committee gave a speech, saying that the disaster in Shaanxi is due to both man-made and natural disasters. However, the fact that the people of various counties in western Shaanxi like to grow opium is an important reason. I will never give up my responsibilities and vow to eradicate this poison. Finally, Nan Ruji reported on accepting Yu's two proposals. Then, they shouted slogans and dispersed. (December 19th)

Negotiations on the Japanese Reporter's Slander of the Harbin Prison

Our Negotiating Representative Lodges a Protest

The Harbin Press Association Investigates the Truth

Harbin Dispatch: Regarding the matter of a Japanese Dentsu News Agency reporter stationed in Harbin fabricating rumors and slandering the prison, on the 18th of this month, the negotiating representative Zhong Yu lodged a protest with the Japanese consul stationed in Harbin. At the same time, the prison authorities sent telegrams to the Capital Judicial Administration Yuan and the Jilin Higher Court, explaining the facts in detail. They also issued a declaration, stating: "The ten articles of the declaration issued by the Japanese Press League on December 16th are pure fabrications. Based on the facts, we refute them as follows. Prisons are executive agencies for criminal defendants and are subject to the review of the original sentencing agency. If a prisoner is ill, the original sentencing agency is notified. If a prisoner dies, it must be examined by an investigating prosecutor. There are registers for the daily entry and exit of prisoners, and records of their daily lives and actions. When they are ill, they are treated by doctors, and after death, their bodies are claimed by their relatives. Even if they are handled by the prison, they must be sent to the charity grounds and buried with markings. The Japanese press declaration falsely accuses prisoner Wang of various situations without specifying which agency sentenced him, where he was buried after death, or the names of the guards who beat the prisoners. If sixty people are on hunger strike for five days, there must be starvation and discontent. Why is it that none of the nine hundred prisoners know about it? On the 10th, Hideaki Kuramoto personally visited and inspected various places. It would be clear at a glance whether prisoners were on hunger strike and whether the prison had other places to house and resist prisoners. The declaration is a complete fabrication and is extremely vile. The accusation that the warden spent three days trying to cover up the matter is also false. On the 11th, 12th, and 13th of this month, people came to the prison every morning, and the warden met them with sincerity, which is enough to show the hypocrisy of the Japanese press. As for the accusation that the afternoon newspaper on the 13th had words criticizing the prison, a full copy of the afternoon newspaper on the 13th has been examined, and it can be seen that the League is fabricating something out of thin air. Motohashi came in person to apologize and drafted a revised telegram, which was translated into Chinese by the secretary Kuramoto. There was no request from the warden. The false accusation of a certain high-ranking Chinese official speaking out should also be pointed out so that it can be proven. This case is of great importance and cannot be resolved by frivolous and unfounded arguments. The Japanese reporter said that he had heard rumors. The declaration also falsely claimed that a high-ranking Chinese official spoke out. In order to clarify the true and accurate facts, we request that those with knowledge of prison studies and law from all countries organize a group to come to the prison to investigate. If it is true, the prison staff will be duly punished. If it is not true, the newspapers affiliated with the Japanese League should also be punished accordingly, so as to show justice to the world. This is the only appropriate course of action." On the afternoon of the 17th, the Harbin Press Association, believing that this matter was of great importance to the recovery of our country's legal rights, sent representatives Zhang Shuping and Lin Xiaotian to visit the prison and the prosecutor's office on the 18th to inquire about the truth and personally entered the prison cells to ask the prisoners about what happened. A report was drafted and submitted to the Press Association for review. (December 20th)

The Soviet Union Prepares to Abolish the Currency System

The Provincial Government Orders Border Counties to Strictly Prevent Infiltration

Jilin Dispatch: Quan Shien, the consul-general stationed in Heihe, Russia, has been reporting on Russian affairs from time to time. Recently, the provincial government received a letter from the consul detailing the Soviet Union's preparations to abolish the currency system. Excerpts are as follows: "Since the implementation of the Soviet Union's New Economic Policy, various industries have been exclusively operated by the state, and the products produced and sold abroad are also government monopolies. As for distribution within the country, private merchants could initially purchase and resell from state-owned stores or the original factories producing the goods. In recent years, the management of state-owned stores in the country has gradually become complete, and their capacity is sufficient to meet the needs of the country. Therefore, they have successively bankrupted private merchants through heavy taxation policies and administrative methods. All stores in urban and rural areas that are not entirely state-owned are jointly operated by the government and certain social organizations. Their business is mainly to distribute various goods to workers in factories and staff in government agencies, and not to make a profit. The method is to designate someone in need to be supplied by a certain official store, and to order the supplied person to pay a certain amount of fees, and then the store will issue a small booklet. In the future, they can use this booklet to receive goods. All those who have obtained this type of booklet are personnel serving in various government agencies and factories. Ordinary merchants and civilians do not have the right to obtain this type of booklet. However, if ordinary people need certain goods and daily necessities, they can exchange them for food, leather, and other raw materials with the Far East National Trade Company or various consumer cooperatives in the countryside. Since this method has been implemented, the use of banknotes in the country has gradually narrowed. In order to prepare for the implementation of the abolition of the currency system and complete absolute communist politics, the Soviet government is now ordering that transactions between various state-owned agencies do not use cash. When various enterprises or agencies have deposits, they must be sent to the National Bank for deposit. For example, when Agency A buys goods from Agency B, it does not directly pay in cash. It only needs the National Bank to deduct the payment from A's deposit and deposit it into B's account, and the transaction is completed. As for the wages of workers in various factories and the salaries of staff in government agencies, it is also planned not to give them cash. The plan is to give them half in food and daily necessities, which they can receive with the small booklet of the official store, and the remaining half of their salary will be deposited by the service agency in the savings bank. It is said that there are no restrictions when withdrawing the money. This is the prelude to the Soviet Union's preparation to abolish the currency system. In recent years, the country's industrial and commercial enterprises have been completely controlled by the government. Transactions between state-owned agencies using cash or being cleared by the bank have the same effect. Furthermore, the Soviet government regards money as a medium for private capital. If state capital occupies the main part of the entire economy, then the function of money has already lost most of its significance. Moreover, for years, state-owned commercial agencies in the country have been exchanging agricultural products and raw materials produced in rural areas for factory products with farmers. Otherwise, no matter how much paper money is given, they will not sell. Paper money has long ceased to have any significant impact on the country's enterprises and economy. Those who use paper money are mostly private capital, but private capital is precisely what communist politics does not tolerate. If private capital is cracked down on, the Soviet government will naturally take resolute measures without hesitation, so long as it does not cause economic panic. This is why the Soviet government is preparing to abolish money. The above is the Soviet Union's domestic situation. If we talk about the external aspect, the Soviet paper currency has been prohibited from leaving the country since it was issued. In theory, there should be no Soviet paper currency abroad. If there is, it is only considered a private currency that has been illegally taken out of the country, and the Soviet Union is not responsible for its exchange. The country's foreign trade, because the major powers do not trust the national paper currency, all demand cash or other countries' redeemable paper currency. Therefore, when the Soviet Union purchases machinery and other types of goods abroad, it uses cash or the foreign currency obtained from the sale of exports as the price for purchasing foreign goods. The Soviet paper currency has never been able to be used conveniently abroad, and even if it is abolished, it will naturally not have any impact on foreign relations. This is the situation of the Soviet Union's economic changes and the trend of the country to abolish the currency system." After receiving the report, the provincial government, fearing that the border areas would be invaded by Soviet private currency and that merchants and civilians would suffer, yesterday issued a special order to all border counties, ordering them to pay close attention to this matter. (December 17th)

Liaoning Province to Establish a Match Monopoly Bureau

Shenyang Dispatch: Zhang Zhenhuai, the Director of Finance, in order to promote domestically produced matches and recover rights and interests, plans to establish a Match Monopoly Bureau. However, since the Northeast prepared for the match monopoly, Japanese merchants have been in a panic. Victory in Suppressing Bandits in Southern Anhui

Over Two Thousand Bandits Dispersed

From Wuhu Communication: In the counties of Langxi, Guangde, and Xuancheng in southern Anhui, dense forests abound. Coupled with last year's drought and hardship for the people, bandits seized the opportunity to secretly establish bogus organizations, coercing and luring good citizens to join their ranks, resulting in bandits everywhere. Although numerous searches and suppressions have been conducted, it has been difficult to completely eliminate them. The bandit leader, Wang Jinlin, is from Guangdong. Recently, he gathered over two thousand bandits, fully armed, and entrenched himself in Tonggou, Taibaogou, and other places. The residents of Langxi and Guangde counties have become a bandit world due to oppression and temptation. A few days ago, they brazenly broke into Xiyao Village in western Guangde, confiscating the guns of the militia, and then attacked the Bai Dian militia, aiming to seize their weapons. Yu Fengrun's entire 342nd Regiment of the 57th Division is stationed in Langxi and Guangde counties. They immediately left two companies to be responsible for the defense of Guangde and Langxi county towns. The remaining twelve infantry companies, as well as mortar and machine gun companies, simultaneously set out from Langxi, Guangde, Shijie Ferry, and other places in several directions, and established contact with the militia, launching a large-scale encirclement. They encountered a large number of bandits in Yaocun and Daliucun, and a conflict ensued. The bandits were driven to Qingfeng Ridge. Unexpectedly, at 2:00 AM the day before yesterday, the bandits, with no way to escape in all directions, suddenly launched a counterattack against Yu's regiment. Yu's regiment also seized the opportunity to bombard them. After a day of fierce fighting and several charges, the bandits finally collapsed on all sides. The bandit leader Wang Jinlin fled in disarray with only forty or fifty men. No less than several hundred bandits were killed by artillery fire. Two wooden cannons, a large number of homemade guns and broadswords were seized, and over forty hostages were rescued. Yu's regiment also lost thirteen soldiers, and two officers were wounded. It was not until yesterday that the various troops returned to their original defenses. All sectors of Guangde specially raised 1,000 yuan to reward the officers and soldiers of the regiment who had contributed. Regiment Commander Yu also telegraphed the details of the bandit suppression to the brigade headquarters of the 171st Brigade stationed in Wuhu. (23rd)

Wuxi

Appeal from Pawnshops in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province. Pawnshops in various counties of Jiangsu Province cite Article 16 of the newly promulgated Jiangsu Provincial Pawnshop Regulations, which states that if the redemption of pawned items is overdue by more than five days, a half-month's interest will be charged, and if it is overdue by more than fifteen days, a month's interest will be charged, with a fixed date of January 1, 1921 for implementation. The Construction Department has instructed pawnshops in various counties to comply. Pawnshops believe that the change to collecting half a month's interest will cause excessive losses to the pawnshop industry and make it unable to sustain itself. Although the Provincial Pawnshop Association has repeatedly fought for this, it has been ineffective. Pawnshop associations in thirteen counties of Jiangsu Province, including Taixing, Dongtai, Wujiang, Kunshan, Songjiang, Dantu, Wuxian, Wujin, Jiangyin, Yixing, Liyang, Changshu, and Wuxi, initiated a letter inviting representatives from pawnshops in various counties to hold a temporary meeting of representatives from pawnshops across the province in the county chamber of commerce on the day before yesterday (the 22nd). They resolved to organize a temporary office for pawnshops in various counties of Jiangsu Province to handle this case, appealing to the province to request a postponement of implementation in order to maintain commercial hardship. The submission of this document to the province was completed yesterday.

Long-distance Telephone Lines in Nine Counties to Establish Three Exchanges in Wuxi. The long-distance telephone lines in nine counties, including Suwu, Xiyi, etc., were being actively prepared by Deng Fubei, Director of the Telecommunications Administration, under the order of the Construction Department. All necessary materials have been purchased and are being carried out separately. Now, Director Deng came to Wuxi the day before yesterday to contact Yao Dixing, Director of the Construction Bureau, believing that the equipment in various counties will be completed soon. It was decided to establish three exchanges in Wuxi, one in the County Government, one in the Public Security Bureau, and one in the Construction Bureau. The telephone poles and lines are planned to be borrowed from the Wuxi Telephone Company.

In the autumn of this year, she was abducted to Xiamen by three men from the factory whose names are unknown and sold to the Xia Yung Ge brothel as a prostitute. The girl, unwilling to engage in the flesh trade, went to the Xiamen Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting assistance. After the county government approved the letter, yesterday a notice was prepared and police were sent to inquire, but there was no household of Chen Jinfu. It is thought that he has moved elsewhere.

The Wuxi Taxation General Office of this county received instructions from the Jiangsu Financial Commissioner's Office the day before yesterday, stating that the subordinate collection agencies should be abolished by December 31, 1921. Changzhou

Military and Police Go to Huangtu to Suppress Bandits. Chuan Zengyi, the company commander of the 7th Company of the 2nd Battalion of the Military Police 2nd Regiment stationed in Wu County, was ordered to go to Huangtu, Jiangyin to suppress bandits on the morning of the 24th at 1:00 AM, together with Chen Tianxi, the police captain. It happened that the bandit leader Xu Linlin forced a kidnapped maiden into marriage at home that day. Comrades and guests filled the house. The military and police went to surround the house and captured Xu and others under the bed in the new house. Xu dared to suddenly rush out and shoot with a gun, attempting to resist arrest and escape. The military police immediately fired back, killing him and dragging him out of the bed. A Mauser pistol and five bullets were found. The military and police, believing that the suspect was indeed a bandit leader, cut off his head and captured eleven accomplices, including Cai Hongqing, in the house. Together with the head, they were taken to the city that afternoon. The police also arrested the bandit suspect Xu Yaoliang in Panshu and brought him to the city together. Xu's head was hung on the gate as a warning to the public. The remaining bandits are under preliminary investigation.

News of County Magistrate's Transfer. Wu Deyao, the magistrate of Wu County, has been in office for nine months. Yesterday (the 24th), news suddenly came from the province that he had been transferred to be the magistrate of Taicang County. The vacancy for the magistrate of Wujin County was filled by Zhang Peng, the magistrate of Siyang County, who was transferred to Changzhou. Upon receiving the news, County Magistrate Wu prepared to conclude all matters.

Jiangyin

Dispute Over Contested Alluvial Land Leads to Litigation. In 1922, the Fuli Company invested in the Duan Shan South Clamp Tapping Garden Beach. The three embankments collapsed, and by May 1923, the company's assets were exhausted. It owed a large sum of money to the mud workers, but had no funds to pay them. Therefore, 7,500 mu of beach land was allocated, with 6,000 mu allocated to the mud workers, one mu per worker as payment, and the remaining 1,500 mu allocated to the mud work foremen and office staff as salaries. Zhu Tingyan represented the negotiations. After the embankment was completed, the weaker mud workers reluctantly sold their land rights to local landlords, and made agreements with the company to designate land sections for collecting rent. However, there are still genuine mud workers who have not sold their land rights for eight years, but still cannot collect rent from even one mu. Therefore, this spring, Zhu Tingyan, as a representative, clarified the boundaries according to the company's records, and the holders of land rights built embankments themselves. Some people, including Zhu Tingqiu, citing the cases of the Houde Company, Tang An, Zhang An, and Xinbao An, accused Zhu Tingyan and others of seizing embankments. The county government repeatedly summoned them for questioning. Now that winter has arrived and the water is low, Zhu Tingyan and others have divided the embankment land and are repairing the banks for each management section. Several dozen mu of land in the East-West beach area of the Chaodong Weigang section head were assigned to Yu Shangyi, Xu Jinxiu, and Wang Chuan to repair the banks. Chen Jiyu, Zhu Jiadong, and Wu Gengyang believe that this hinders their new case, and have filed a complaint with the county accusing Zhu Tingyan, Yu Shangyi, and others of seizing the embankment. On the 23rd, the county summoned them for questioning. Zhu Jiadong and others stated that the area Zhu Tingyan was embanking was the area they had reported in 1926, had received land ownership certificates, and had repeatedly reported to the county, requesting the police to order a stop to the construction, but the report was ignored and the construction continued. Ding Shipu, commissioned by Zhu Tingyan, and Yu Shangyi and others stated that the embankment area was the address reported by the Fuli Company, and they had submitted it to the Sandfield General Bureau and forwarded it to the two provincial governors of Jiangsu, informing the Ministry of Finance to restrict the reporting of new cases by a second company or individual. Chen Jiyu reported the case in 1926, four years after the settlement of the Fuli embankment case, and the location was also within the scope, which was an illegal seizure. They also submitted a detailed map of the boundary. The court ordered a further summons for questioning.

Court Hearing of the Case of the Market Strike by Merchants and Residents in Ligang. In Ligang Town, 6th District, the merchants and residents went on strike because Gu Shijia, the leader of the 1st Squad of the County Police Force stationed there, used plainclothes police to arrest gamblers. On the 23rd, the county government summoned Deputy Regiment Commander Xu Qin'an, Squad Leader Gu Shijia, and patrol officers Ding Changqing and Liu Tongfa for questioning. Xu Qin'an testified that at 10:00 AM on November 27th, plainclothes police came to the town to arrest gamblers. He happened to be coming out of the store and asked what was happening. He was then beaten by patrol officers Ding Changchun and Liu Tongfa, and lost 40 yuan in banknotes, 5 yuan in silver, 10 dimes in small silver coins, and 35 copper coins from his pocket. Gu Shijia testified that he was stationed in Chouzhuang because he heard that bandits were entering Ligang along the river from the river mouth, so he set up sentries in the area. There was a gambling den in a teahouse, and the plainclothes police entered to question them. Suddenly, Lu Liben, the patrol leader of the Second Police Station of the Sixth Sub-bureau, ordered the patrol officer Deng Deyu to beat the plainclothes police. Xu Qin'an and others argued with him, so he brought them back to the squad but did not beat them. Patrol officers Ding Changqing and Liu Tongfa gave roughly the same testimony. After the questioning, they were ordered to return and await a further summons for questioning. However, Cao Zongduo, the Chief of the Sixth District, mediated in the case and ordered the plaintiffs to withdraw and settle peacefully.

Several Hundred Hakkas Suddenly Arrive in Huangtu. Since Cao Zongduo took office as the Chief of the District and Jin Junxu took office as the Chief of the District Regiment in the Western Countryside, the bandit atmosphere there has calmed down slightly. However, robberies still occur from time to time in the northern countryside of Wujin. Yesterday (the 24th), several hundred people who resembled Hakkas suddenly arrived in Huangtu, wandering around in the town, similar to those meeting bandits. The town chief, fearing other developments as winter defense was approaching, sent Nian Zu to the Xia Port telephone station in the evening to report to the Public Security Bureau, requesting proper precautions. County Magistrate Li had gone to the province yesterday morning, and Director Li reported it to Secretary Xu for handling.

Nantong

The Re-division of Police Districts in the Entire County. The police districts in Nantong County are re-divided according to the autonomous regions, with a total of 19 sub-bureaus. The appointed bureau chiefs are as follows: Li Laiqin in the urban area, Zhu Yiqing in Tangzha, Chen Renzhi in Pingchao, Li Hanhui in Liuqiao, Shi Deyun in Guanren, Ding Daochang in Sian, Zhang Songting in Shigang, Gao Yi in Xiting, Wu Fuqiang in Jinsha, Xiao Guogan in Jinghua, Song Boang in Yuxi, Tang Heling in Yiyi, Fan Kang in Yudong, Jiang Xuemei in Lusi, Du Yutian in Liuhaisha, Chen Duo in Baipu, Zhang Shushen in Kenmu, Chen Xingshao in Sanyu, and Tang Ruiquan in Gangbu. There are also 14 sub-stations, with Yang Xianyu, etc. appointed as patrol officers. The expenses of each bureau and station will be allocated by the County Bureau in the future, and self-financing is strictly prohibited.

Implementation of Township Clearance. The Township Clearance affairs of Tongyi were suspended due to bandit suppression. They are ordered by the province to continue, and at the same time, a household census is being carried out, with Ding Ziyan appointed as the director.

Rugao

Bandits Active Again on the Border of Tongru. In the area of Zhentao and Pingchao on the border of Tongru, the bandits who fled to other places some time ago have returned to their villages one after another, and are carrying out large-scale activities. The night before last, dozens of communist bandits in Xinlu, southwest of Pingchao District, opened fire with Mauser pistols to demonstrate, firing about one hundred and several dozen shots. The villagers, who had just calmed down, were plunged into panic again.

Sea Bandits Rampant, Burning Boats. The sea pirates in Juegang are in a state of panic because of the daily shortage of thatch, water, and oil. Today (the 20th), the pirate ships in Nankan Port actually chopped up the fishing boats of Ge Yufang and others, which were parked in the port, and used them as fuel, and went to the nearby area to fetch fresh water. Therefore, the fishermen in each place are afraid of being kidnapped and dare not go there. They are now in a state of sealing the sea.

Zhenjiang

Political Police Officer Accused of Beating the Director. Han Ziping, the director of the Zhenjiang County Prison, was beaten by officers. He went to the court to request an examination of the injuries, which were confirmed to be true. He was ordered to seek medical treatment at his own expense and await a warrant to appear in court.

Complaint Against the Magistrate of Yangzhou County. Wang Chuan Dao, a citizen of Yangzhou County, previously accused Magistrate Xu of the county of taking bribes to release bandits to the provincial government. Yesterday, the Department of Civil Affairs summoned Wang Chuan Dao and transferred him to the court for investigation according to law, and then summoned Xu to confront him.

Soliciting Donations for Construction Bonds. The County Government has scheduled a meeting on the 29th of this month to convene the gentry, wealthy people, and chairmen of various trade associations to discuss the allocation of construction bonds.

Confiscation of Ma Yuren's Property. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs previously received an order from the magistrate of Yancheng County to confiscate the property of bandit Ma Yuren and those who joined Ma in creating turmoil to offset the post-disaster expenses. Although the national government had issued a clear order to arrest bandit Ma, there was no indication of confiscating his property. The post-disaster affairs in the disaster-stricken areas of Yanfu require urgent funds. It is proposed to first confiscate all the property to offset the expenses before Ma is arrested. A special report was submitted to the provincial government for instructions. The provincial government instructed to do so. However, the part of those who joined the bandits must be handled separately. The county has been ordered to comply yesterday, and also ordered to report the handling situation.

Yangzhou

Escorting and Ordering the Disbanding of Officers Out of the Country. The Enforcing Law Team of the Headquarters of the 94th Brigade stationed in Yangzhou checked the hotels last night and found four armed men, Ma Ganquan and others, in Rooms 20 and 21 of the Dalu Hotel on Xin Sheng Street, claiming to be officers of a certain disbanded division who were returning home through this port. The team checked Ma and others and found no other illegal activities, so they ordered them to remove their weapons, settle the room fees, and escorted them out of the country.

The Pacification Commissioner's Office Arrests Suspects. The Pacification Supervisory Office received a secret report that a guest named Gu Wenhua was staying at the Yingzhou Hotel on Gengzi Street in this city, suspected of a certain crime. The Military Law Office of the Office sent a team to check, but they did not find him. Later, they learned that Gu was hiding in the home of Chen Yuming at No. 33 Dicang Lane. The team went there with the police officers of the Public Security Bureau at 10:00 PM last night (the 23rd) and arrested Gu Wenhua and Chen Yuming together, and found a set of smoking paraphernalia. It was heard that the Military Law Office considered opium smoking a judicial matter and sent Gu Wenhua to the court, and Chen Yuming was handed over to the Public Security Bureau to be guarded and investigated.

Request to Build the Embankment According to the Old Route. Xu Shaotang and others, who manage the fields of the Nursery in this county, reported that Zhang Fangyun, a technician from the Construction Bureau, was measuring the Yangyi Road with rural officials and villagers and planting wooden stakes in the fields owned by the Nursery in Yujia Camp for the route. It was found that the last measurement was a straight line from east to west on the north side of the field, but now the stakes are being planted in a bow shape in the low fields for no reason. The Nursery specially submitted a request to the county government yesterday, asking the Construction Bureau to build the embankment according to the old route to avoid damage to the Nursery's fields.

Yangzhou

The Provincial Commission Supervises the Compilation of the Defense Corps. The Jiangsu Department of Civil Affairs believes that the Baojia movement is extremely important during the period of political tutelage, and bandit alarms are frequently heard as winter approaches. Hu Gui, a special commissioner of the Provincial Garrison Area Defense Corps, was sent to Yangzhou to supervise the compilation. Mr. Hu was sent from Zheng to Yangzhou on the evening of the 22nd. On the morning of the 23rd, he went to the county government to discuss everything with County Magistrate Xu, and went to the County Party Department to meet with the Wang Tang committee members to discuss the promotion. It is heard that their implementation plan is to establish at least one team in each district first, and they will go to each district with the county magistrate in the coming days to convene township heads and order the supervision of the compilation. Mr. Hu will stay here for a week. Once the supervision of the compilation is completed, he will go to Jiangdu to handle it.

Hangzhou

Planning the Establishment of a Provincial Livestock Farm. The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining, in view of the many uses of cattle, is now planning to start setting up a provincial livestock improvement farm and cattle breeding department. The estimated cost of the project was previously estimated to be 76,500 yuan for start-up expenses and 56,200 yuan for recurring expenses, which are planned to be provided by the provincial funds.

Ningbo

Municipal Government Reduces Expenses, Implements Staff Reductions. The Ningbo Municipal Government has been ordered by the province to earnestly reduce expenses. Because the administrative expenses have been reduced, the government has no choice but to implement staff reductions. Therefore, starting yesterday, two staff members from the Health Section, one administrative staff member, two assistant secretaries from the Secretariat, and one clerk were dismissed to save expenses.

The Water Patrol Team Seizes Another Large Group of Pirates. The patrol ships and patrol teams under the Zhenhai Water Police Bureau have repeatedly captured pirates in recent days. The Fifth Water Patrol Team of the Bureau captured seven pirates, Weng Simei, Jiang Xiaomei, Huang Xiaoyu, Lin Zengbao, Bi Laowu, Luo Mei, and Weng Huatian, and rescued one refugee, Jin Jinbang, and seized 13 rifles and 205 bullets on the sea off Huanghua, Wenzhou. The Sixth and Seventh Water Patrol Teams captured six pirates, Liu Xuesheng, Wang Yizheng, Pan Wenchou, Zhu Rongsheng, Wu Rongfa, and Wang Xiangan, in the sea off Jinqing Port, Haimen. The pirates captured by the three teams were escorted to Zhenhai by the Nanhai ship and handed over to the Water Police Bureau for verification and handling yesterday afternoon.

The Young Master of the Stone Factory Kidnapped. Xu Hong, a resident of Kong of Lujiabu Lishan, Cixi, who opened the Hongsheng Stone Factory, was suddenly kidnapped by six or seven bandits the day before yesterday evening, demanding a ransom of 5,000 yuan. The meeting point was set at the Jiusong Pavilion in Nanhuang. Xu only has this one son and is extremely saddened after being kidnapped. He is now trying to find a way to redeem him.

Hefei

The Defense of Hefei Amidst the Rampant Communist Bandits in Luan. The headquarters of the 46th Division and the county government here received a telegram from Luan stating that a large number of communist bandits are rampant in the western countryside of the county. The regiments of the 46th Division stationed in Luan and those heading from Fei are advancing to suppress them on the 19th. However, because He Lu is close, Chairman Chen has transferred the 1st Guard Brigade of Shi Zhongcheng, stationed in Qianshan, to Fei on the night of the 16th to assist in the defense. He also ordered Wang stationed in Wu the 171st Brigade of the 57th Division to open to Fei. The County Government of Fei publicly announced this news on the 20th to reassure the people, and ordered the chiefs of each regiment in Kunlian and Liu Jing in the Western Countryside to contact each other and block them as opportunity serves.

The Radio Station Begins to Broadcast. The Construction Department sent technician Xia Cangyi to Fei to install a radio station in the Houjin of Changhan Village on Xiaodongmen Avenue, considering Hefei an important town in central Anhui. The installation was completed on the 18th, and broadcasting began on the 19th to Shanghai, Nanjing, Hankou, Nanchang, Bengbu, and other places. Technician Xia has already returned to the province to report.

Special Report on Education News

Research Report of the Children's Life Guidance Group of the Jiangsu Provincial United Elementary School (1)

Report by Hu Shuyi, Nanjing Women's Middle School Experimental Elementary School

I. A Small Introduction

Entrusted with the mission of the previous conference to make a comprehensive report on the acquisition of research on children's life guidance,

Due to limited time, this adult's problem of children's life guidance can only be given a small and simple report.

We respectfully dedicate the acquisition of research on children's life guidance to the research and reference of all instructors with the utmost enthusiasm.

Naturally, there are no major discoveries in this report that can be contributed, nor are there profound theories that can be deeply explored. There are only the research acquisition facts of the process, regardless of right and wrong, truthfully written below for the deep study and review of all instructors. At the same time, we sincerely look forward to some rigorous criticisms from teachers who like to study children's life guidance.

II. A Historical Observation of Children's Autonomy

Education in the era before children were discovered can be simply summarized in one sentence: Children receiving education was akin to sitting in prison. From the education that maintained royal families, nobles, monks, and the privileges of the upper class, to the Spartan education that preserved national prosperity, and even to the education of individualism with religious colors, all are examples of disregarding children's education. These are undeniable historical traces.

It was 校 (JEAUJACUESROUSSEAU), a person drunk with the beauty of nature and active in the love of human life, who introduced children to the field of education. It was not until the beginning of this century, with Ellen Key (ELLENKTY) of Northern Europe and her child-centered education, that children were discovered. Rousseau wrote "Emile," advocating nature and strongly criticizing the fallacies of previous education. Our dear children were then noticed by educators. Key wrote "The Century of the Child," deeply lamenting the decline of family education and loudly advocating for the reform of school education. Only then did a ripple of child-centeredness appear in the educational thought trends.

However, the facts tell us that from the end of the eighteenth century to the beginning of the twentieth century, although a trend of children's education and a ripple of child-centeredness were discovered in our field, the general children were still the same as before. Except for some slight reforms in schools, everything else remained the same as before, or perhaps it could be said, almost the same.

In the midst of the high-pitched call for the century of the child, in the past decade, the education circles in China have mostly been managing children's autonomy to adapt to the approaching call of the century of the child, the educational trend of child-centeredness.

Here, we want to make a general review and strict criticism of the current general children's autonomy.

The lifeless Chinese education circles do not need blindly flattering criticism. We really want to expose the diseases of children's autonomy in principle, organization, and implementation, which may serve as a wake-up call for those who have gone astray.

Honestly speaking, exposing the morbid state is also a tool for research.

1. Morbid State in Principle

A. Separation of discipline and instruction: a part of education is carved out to manage children's autonomy. The school hires a disciplinarian to be solely responsible for the cultivation of children's character, and hires several teachers to specially teach children some book knowledge. Thus, discipline and instruction go their separate ways.

Activity is a tool for children to acquire knowledge, and experimentation is a means to complete experience. May I ask if this activity that separates discipline and instruction can satisfy children's lives?

News

Ministry of Education's Handover and Acceptance Situation

The newly appointed political and vice ministers of the Ministry of Education took office on the 22nd. The situation has been recorded in this newspaper. The following is a brief summary of the handover of ministerial affairs by the former minister and the acceptance by the new minister, based on what the reporter has learned.

Huge Surplus of Funds Handed Over

Since the establishment of the Ministry of Education two years ago, due to savings in expenditures and fewer personnel than other ministries (the total number of members is less than one hundred), there was a monthly surplus in the original budget. The ministry's premises were narrow and insufficient for use, so the surplus funds were used to purchase land and build two buildings, one for the offices of the various departments and one for the auditorium and library. Both buildings were strongly built and well-equipped, with running water and water heaters. The installation was completed only on the 20th of this month. On the day the new minister arrived, the rooms were brand new. The construction cost a total of more than 100,000 yuan. Although the funds had been requested from the Executive Yuan as temporary expenses, they had not been received due to the insufficient national treasury. Therefore, the daily surplus funds were used for construction needs. When the handover was made, excluding the construction costs that had already been paid, the accumulated surplus funds due to the non-payment of funds by the Ministry of Finance were very large. It has now been handed over to the new minister for acceptance.

Telegram to Chairman Chiang Reporting the Acceptance Situation

All existing members of the Ministry of Education, except for the minister, vice minister, secretary director Zheng Tianting, and head of the document section Zhang Ying, have been handed over to the new minister. After the new two vice ministers arrived at the ministry, in addition to inviting Councilor Zhao Naiquan to concurrently serve as secretary and secretary director, and newly appointing the heads of the first, second, third, and fourth sections of the General Affairs Department and two secretaries (the list has been recorded in the previous newspaper), yesterday, He Jinghuang was announced as a member of the Secretariat, Li Xiaolou as a member of the General Education Department, Wang Xuesu, Jing Tong, Zhang Chongzhi, and Zan Wen as members of the General Affairs Department. As for the acceptance of ministerial affairs, Zhao Naichuan and others were appointed as acceptance officers. After Zhao and others were dispatched, they held a meeting that day to discuss the acceptance methods. The result was that each department and office first prepared a handover list, and then the acceptance officers checked the list. In reality, since the existing members of the ministry had not changed much, the so-called handover and acceptance was only a formal procedure that could not be avoided. Yesterday (24th), in addition to submitting a report to the Executive Yuan on the date of the oath of office, the new two vice ministers also telegraphed Chairman Jiang to report the situation, and stated that they had followed the instructions of Your Excellency and retained all the officials of the various departments and offices except for slight changes in the General Affairs Department and the Secretariat, and that ministerial affairs were proceeding as usual.

Ministry of Education Promotes Phonetic Symbols

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, attaching a small booklet on the practice of phonetic symbols, ordering them to instruct their subordinates to actually promote phonetic symbols and widely publicize them. At the same time, it also requested the Ministry of Interior to instruct the Capital Police Department to add phonetic symbols to the nameplates of streets and alleys in the capital.

Ministry of Education Orders Shandong Province to Plan Vocational Education for the Whole Province

Vocational Schools That Have Been Suspended Should Be Restored Quickly

Those That Are Already in Operation Should Be Expanded Vigorously

The Shandong Education Department submitted a proposal to the Ministry of Education to reorganize provincial schools. Regarding the suspension of vocational schools, the Ministry of Education, after receiving the report, yesterday issued an instruction to the department to make a comprehensive plan for vocational schools, to quickly restore those that have been suspended, and to vigorously expand those that are currently in operation, or to establish vocational subjects in various middle schools to make up for the deficiencies. The original order stated:

The report and the list of circumstances have been fully understood. The department's intention to investigate the management of various schools and plan for improvement is very good. The methods listed in items 2 to 7 of the list are also very feasible. However, item 1 proposes to suspend all three existing provincial second, fourth, and fifth vocational schools. It is true that the equipment of each school is simple and the results are too poor. However, vocational education is related to the lives of young people and the livelihoods of vocational citizens, and is extremely important. At present, most middle and primary school graduates want to go to higher education, but they suffer from a lack of financial resources. They want to be independent, but they suffer from a lack of specialized skills. They are in a dilemma and do not know where to go. The weak become decadent and sink, while the strong tend to go astray. The society is chaotic and has no end. All of this is due to the great underdevelopment of vocational education. The local authorities handle vocational education, limited by economic and human resources, and often the spirit is completely different. It is necessary to raise funds widely, recruit talents, earnestly supervise, and promote at any time. Those with excessively poor results and unable to be reorganized should be suspended and reorganized to actively proceed. If, after the suspension, the students are dismissed and completely canceled, it is inevitable that one will choke while eating. How can we abandon the malpractices and promote education? The plan to improve secondary education decided at the second National Education Conference this year stipulates the ratio of the number of ordinary high schools to agricultural and industrial high schools in items 1 and 2 of section C of the method for setting up middle schools, which shows the urgent need for vocational education. The department must make a comprehensive plan for vocational education based on the situation in the province, quickly restore those that have been suspended, and vigorously expand those that are currently in operation, or establish vocational subjects in various middle schools to make up for the deficiencies. Please follow the instructions and report the matter with a list. This order.

Miller, Weitema, Lihm, Feidan, Johnson

Chen Yutian Exploded out of Nowhere

Lehua kicked off and was obtained by the enemy. From the middle to the right, Zhou Xianyan waited patiently, and then counterattacked, but was unable to advance due to offside. Lehua made a concerted effort, and the momentum was still good. At six or seven minutes, Chen Yutian flew fast and rushed into the right side quickly. About ten yards from the goal, he raised his foot and attacked from a distance. Goalkeeper Mars was unable to jump up and the enemy's goal was broken. The audience cheered. Based on this situation, it is unbelievable that Lehua would have such a miserable defeat.

Penalty Kicks Were Repeatedly Awarded to the Enemy

Just when it was thought that Lehua might have a glimmer of hope today, the enemy's center Lihm Fei knocked on the door alone after 25 minutes of the game. The defense was unsuccessful and it became a tie. Since then, the British army's momentum suddenly became stronger, and they moved freely from left to right, doing whatever they wanted. The ball came from Kai Gen and the left winger Miller, and then to the center Henm Fei three times. Zhou Xianyan was helpless, and Lehua lost by 1 to 2. Li Ning was blocking the enemy when the referee ruled that he had fouled and awarded a penalty kick. Right Guard Biquin rushed over and kicked it in. With the loss of vitality, Lehua was beyond help. The British army's right winger Johnson flew in from the right and kicked a ball diagonally from 30 yards away from the goal, hitting the corner of the net. Lehua lost by 1 to 4 in the first half.

Zhou Yanxian Became the Target of Public Criticism

Changing sides and fighting again, Lehua was still in decline and unable to recover. With one move, the ball was immediately in the hands of the enemy. One person fought against three or four people, and the threat was immediately at the door. There was always the risk of losing the goal. The ball was only a few inches away from the goal, and it was not uncommon. Surrounded by attacks on the goal, Zhou Xianyan became the target of public criticism. Defending against a barrage of artillery fire, it was not a matter for a veteran of the iron gate. The falling flowers and flowing water were unbearable to look back on. Dan's attack made it 5 to 1, and Weitema connected with Miller's corner kick to make it 6 to 1. Dan scored again to make it 7 to 1. The continuous loss of goals cannot be recorded.

Chen Yutian Desperately Broke Through the Enemy's Goal

After suffering a crushing defeat, the audience dispersed one after another. Only more than ten minutes were left until the end of the game. Wang Shusen was injured and left the field. The remnants of the army fought hard and launched a desperate battle. They had the heart to attack the goal, but the ball did not go in. Suddenly, Chen Yutian went from the right again, 30 yards away from the goal, and flew diagonally from the right towards the goal. The enemy's goal was broken again, and they were able to regain another goal. The contribution of Chen, who had not completely overturned the entire army, was great. Afterwards, Weitema scored another goal for the enemy, making it 8 to 2 and ending the game.

Local News

Yesterday's Commemoration of the Yunnan Uprising Assembly

Numerous Representatives from All Circles Attended

The Shanghai Special City Party Department Executive Committee of the City Party Department convened representatives from all circles at 9:00 AM yesterday in the Party Department's third floor to hold a commemoration assembly for the 15th anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising. Over one hundred groups attended, with a total of over seven hundred representatives. Various townships and districts also held commemoration ceremonies separately. Details of each are recorded below.

Assembly Staff: Chairman Yang Qingyuan, Recorder Zhou Hanmei, Master of Ceremonies Xu Yefu, Reception Zhang Hanyun, Chen Ming, Jiang Zhenwu, Yuan Qingping.

Attending Representatives: Mao Yun from the China Law Society, He Yuanming from the Shanghai Law College Alumni Association, Lu Dafu and Yu Mingzhang from the Shanghai Shipbuilding Industry Union, Han Zongyi and Yang Sili from the Postal Administration, Tang Junsheng from the China Business Electrical Workers' Union, Yang Zheng from the City Social Bureau, Xu Menglin from the Business Union, and representatives from over one hundred other groups, totaling over seven hundred people.

Chairman's Report: Respected representatives, esteemed comrades, today is the 15th anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising. It was because Yuan Shikai declared himself emperor, abolishing the Republic of China, that our Party comrades launched the Yunnan Uprising on December 25th of the fourth year of the Republic of China. Yuan was the most ambitious of the warlords of the past, holding the greatest military power during the Qing Dynasty. While still a subject of the Qing court, he already harbored the ambition to usurp the throne. When the Xinhai Revolution broke out, he seized the opportunity to usurp the Republic of China. He violated the Premier's principles by assuming office in Beijing, then proceeded to suppress revolutionary forces and oppress revolutionary comrades, presumptuously declaring himself emperor. Yuan's imperial ambitions were fueled by his own insatiable desires, and abetted by the sycophantic flattery of individuals like Yang Du. At that time, although democratic politics were surging worldwide, the Chinese people's understanding was immature and they lacked political awareness. Therefore, when Yuan declared himself emperor, the masses were largely ignorant and confused. Simultaneously, imperialists, taking advantage of the ongoing European War, sought to dominate China. Yuan, in this confluence of circumstances, actually realized his imperial dream. At the time, the Premier knew that Yuan could not be loyal to the Republic of China, so while out of office, he contacted revolutionary comrades, secretly uniting them and planning the overthrow of Yuan. Thus, thirteen days after Yuan's imperial proclamation, Yunnan issued its final ultimatum to Yuan on December 23rd, demanding the restoration of the Republic of China and the execution of Yang Du and others. Yuan, of course, did not issue an order accepting this proposal, and Yunnan declared independence, formally launching the campaign against Yuan. Yuan, initially deceived by those around him, realized he had made a terrible mistake and died in remorse and anger. Therefore, summing up the facts of the Yunnan Uprising, it can be said to be a struggle between feudal forces and democratic forces. As a result of the struggle, democratic forces ultimately prevailed. Now, the Republic of China has been unified, and the Party's power has extended throughout the country. Feudal warlords like Yan and Feng have also been eliminated. However, feudal forces in various regions remain exceptionally rampant. Corruption among officials and the tyranny of local bullies are frequently heard of. It must be understood that feudal forces are built upon land capital. Unless the land problem is thoroughly resolved, it will be difficult to eradicate feudal forces. The Fourth Plenary Session resolved to first eliminate the communist bandits. This is certainly a very important task, because after the bandits are eliminated, the people can live and work in peace. But, according to the facts, even if the bandits are eliminated, many people will still have no place to live in peace and no work to enjoy, because fundamentally, many farmers have no land to cultivate. Therefore, in the future, it is hoped that the central government will pay attention to this and thoroughly resolve the land problem, realizing the Premier's legacy of "land to the tiller." Then, the livelihood problems of the farmers, who account for over 80% of China's population, can be solved, and the Chinese revolution can be completed without going astray, because feudal forces are built on land capital. Then, after the land problem is resolved, economic equality can be achieved, and political equality can be completed. The Fourth Plenary Session paid full attention to the development of industry. However, to achieve the goal of developing industry, attention should be paid to the purchasing power of the people. Assuming that the people's purchasing power is strong, the development of industry will not be a major problem. If the people's livelihood is difficult, no matter how much we advocate domestic goods and develop industry, the result will still be empty talk. Therefore, whether or not the land problem is resolved is not only the key to whether feudal forces are eradicated, but also the key to the development of industry. The second point is to overthrow imperialism. This issue is almost a commonplace by now. But in reality, the distance between the Chinese revolution and the overthrow of imperialism is still very distant. At the same time, as long as imperialism exists, the Chinese revolution cannot be completed. Among the international imperialists, the one that invades China most urgently and severely is the Japanese imperialists. Forty-five percent of their country's products are sold to China. Therefore, Japanese imperialists least want the Chinese revolution to succeed, to have a peaceful, unified, and strong central government. Therefore, we should recognize that Japan is the greatest enemy of the Chinese revolution. To complete the Chinese revolution, to make China's international status equal, economic status equal, and political status equal, we must first overthrow Japanese imperialism. The first step in overthrowing Japanese imperialism is to boycott Japanese goods. If the Chinese people fully adopt domestic goods and boycott foreign goods, its effectiveness can strike a fatal blow to Japanese imperialism. Other European and American countries, their ambitions to seize the Chinese market, have intensified their attacks due to their own economic panic. Therefore, to overthrow international imperialists, we should boycott foreign goods, resolutely and persistently adopt economic severance measures. Today is the commemoration of the Yunnan Uprising. When we think back to the difficulty of creating the Republic of China and the multitude of enemies of the Republic of China, now that the country is unified, we cannot help but learn from the past and be careful in the future. I offer these two points to encourage the representatives present, hoping that everyone will earnestly do it. Finished.

Summary of Speeches: First, Chen Kecheng gave a speech, roughly saying: On this commemoration day of the Yunnan Uprising, listening to the chairman's report, I cannot help but have some thoughts to share with the representatives present. Eradicating feudal forces is indeed a serious problem for our country's revolution today. The purpose of the Local Autonomy Training Institute established by the municipal government is to ensure that future municipal administration is not usurped by corrupt local bullies, but is driven by the efforts of revolutionary comrades. But eradicating feudal forces is by no means something that can be accomplished solely through local autonomy. Other efforts still depend on the struggle of our Party comrades and the general revolutionary masses. Then, Yang Sili, Jin Xihan, Liang Wenfa, etc., gave speeches in succession. The length of the speeches is omitted.

Various County Organs: The joint commemoration of the Yunnan Uprising by various organs of Shanghai County was held yesterday at 9:00 AM in the auditorium of the county government. All personnel from various organs attended. Jiang Yanqiu, the propaganda minister of the County Consolidation Committee, presided over the meeting, led the attendees in saluting, and reported on the course of the Yunnan Uprising and its significance. Then, County Magistrate Yan Shenyu and others gave speeches in succession. Finally, slogans were shouted and the meeting adjourned.

Navy Special Party Department: Yesterday was the 15th anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising. The Navy Special City Party Department, together with the Shanghai-based Navy, held a commemoration assembly at 10:00 AM in the department's auditorium. Dozens of people attended. Ren Guangyu presided over the meeting, and Cai Linbing reported on the history of the Yunnan Uprising and the significance of our commemoration. The ceremony concluded at 11:00 AM.
