Icing sugar opens extremely briskly. Over 1,000 bags of new green sugar are flooding in.

Yesterday, there were no telegrams from the sugar production areas due to the Christmas holiday. Market sentiment at the Exchange was quite good, and sales have turned active. Demand is increasing in various parts of the interior. The Changzhou and Wuxi areas are particularly eager to buy sugar because the implementation of the unified tax has increased costs. As a result, market prices are gradually rising. The rapid pace of this trend has been rare in recent years. At the beginning of the market, Dutch sugar (24 degree coarse white sugar) rose by 8 taels and 9 cents, with 500 bags traded, but there was a shortage of sellers and strong buying interest. Prices rose to 9 taels, and trading became more active. High-quality sugar reached 9 taels and 9 cents, and the market was quite firm. 18-degree medium white sugar was priced at 8 taels and 3 cents, and 20-degree sugar was priced at 8 taels and 5 cents, with few buyers. Dutch brown sugar also rose sharply at the same time, with 8-degree sugar priced at 7 taels and 7 cents to 7.5 cents, 9-degree sugar at 7 taels and 8.5 cents, and even 10-degree sugar rose to 8 taels. The market was also not weak. Japanese sugar prices rose even more sharply, and trading was very busy. The market was extremely chaotic. At the beginning of the market, YT grade was priced at 8 taels and 8 cents, then immediately rose to 9 taels. YRO grade was priced at 8 taels and 4 cents, YP grade was priced at 9 taels and 3 to 9 taels and 4 cents, Meiji sugar was priced at 9 taels and 4 to 5 cents, TM grade was priced at 8 taels and 7 cents, and TK grade was priced at 8 taels and 8 cents to 9 taels and 5 cents. Buying interest was still strong, and later prices were called up by one cent, but there were few inquiries. The market was very firm. Nanyang Factory opened the market with over 200 bags of this factory's rock sugar, with grade 1 priced at 11 taels and 3 cents, and grade 2 at 11 taels and 1 cent, a sudden increase of 2 cents compared to the previous session. At the same time, Shanghai Factory also raised prices, and prices are expected to rise again. The icing sugar market also opened higher, with Yuxiang, Yufa, and Jinxing Factories each opening with 500-600 bags, priced at 7 taels and 7.5 to 7 taels and 8 cents, and high-quality sugar at 7 taels and 9.5 cents, totaling over 1,000 bags, and the market was quite brisk. Since the arrival of a large shipment of domestic new green sugar from Zesheng the day before yesterday, over 1,000 bags were opened yesterday, priced at 2 taels and 8 cents, a gradual decrease of 2 cents compared to the previous session, but the market seemed quite stable.

Silk and Tea: Double Palace Silk Sales Clear, Prices Weak

The current market only opens at 470 taels, a decrease of 20 taels compared to the previous session. The Double Palace Silk market in this port has seen market prices gradually rise due to smooth sales of domestic silk fabrics, with a very rapid upward trend. The price of high-quality Double Palace Silk rose from 420 taels to 490 taels. Recently, with the Shanghai port's silk transported to Zhejiang and Jiangsu, the government has approved duty-free passage, and sales of Double Palace Silk machines have been greatly affected. In addition, with the approach of the New Year and the clearer sales appetite of silk merchants, silk prices have gradually fallen. The current price of high-quality Double Palace Silk is only 470 taels, a decrease of 20 taels compared to the previous fall.

The Most Scarce and Popular Textiles and Woolens Recently

Including Sea Tiger Velvet, etc. (four or five kinds)

Recently, due to the cold weather, transactions in wool and woolen goods have been very brisk, and the number of orders received by shops for custom-made coats has increased sharply. Tailors are rushing to complete orders day and night. General wholesale transactions seem to be slightly quieter, perhaps due to the approaching New Year. However, there are many goods that are in short supply, prices are rising, and buyers are in urgent need of them, such as Sea Tiger velvet, Melton cloth, camel wool, 1.6-foot velvet, and gray felt cloth. Buyers have recently been eager to purchase these goods, but most of them have already been sold out and are difficult to find. Yesterday, Sea Tiger grade was sold at around 8 or 9 taels, and camel wool was priced at 7 taels, 5 or 6 cents, but they were hard to come by. Melton cloth, which was sold for 1 tael and 5 cents at the beginning of autumn, is now difficult to obtain even at 2 taels, 4 or 5 cents. Shoe manufacturers are making every effort to find 1.6-foot velvet and gray felt cloth, and sales prices have increased by 2 or 3 cents. In addition, lower-grade 1 tael, 7 or 8 cents of mixed-color serge, single-sided Yuan Zhigong cloth, and various types of fancy cloth and mandarin jacket cloth priced at 4 taels are also in very short supply. Those in the industry with ample funds are eager to buy and stockpile these goods because it is expected that the spring textile and woolen market will improve significantly due to the current tight exchange rates and the upcoming increase in import duties.

Qing Yuan (Green Field)

An Impression of Jiming Temple (by Qing Yu)

It was exactly the third day of my arrival in Nanjing when Fu Dong came to visit me. Upon meeting, we felt an indescribable emotion. If you call it happiness, after three years of separation, we had both experienced unexpected changes, and our appearances had also changed considerably. We were also filled with unknowable conjectures about the future. If you call it sadness, we were both still alive upon meeting, so why be sad? For a moment, we both suppressed the words we wanted to pour out. No, at this moment, we couldn't explain it. We suppressed the surging emotions in our hearts and maintained a normal attitude. Fu Dong asked me why I came.

(I've wanted to come to this place for a long time. In addition, the great upheaval caused by bandits in my hometown forced me to move, so I came here.)

Actually, I don't feel much flavor here, but at least I'm a little less frightened.

(Isn't that also suitable for my purpose? I also just want to rest from the shock. But isn't this an old city? A new capital? The relics of the past, the emerging constructions, the scenic mountains and rivers, I can all admire them.)

(Okay, come along, you'll know for yourself, but that's all there is to it, don't be too excited.)

He spoke without much excitement, but then continued,

(We've been separated for too long, so of course we should spend the whole day together today. But how would you like to spend this precious day?)

(It's up to you to arrange it, I'm a newcomer here.)

(Let's go to Jiming Temple to spend the day, we need to pour everything out to each other as much as possible.)

With that, we came out and headed towards Beijige. It wasn't very far from Huangnigang to Beijige, so naturally we arrived in a while. Under the gloomy weather, after passing through a newly renovated but desolate road that seemed to be a forest but felt too monotonous, we began to climb the mountain. At this time, sparse raindrops had already begun to fall. There was no one else on the mountain road, only the sound of rain on the leaves harmonizing with our soft conversation. After turning two or three bends, we glimpsed a few dilapidated statues of gods, and then we arrived at the temple gate. At the temple gate stood a man in gray clothes carrying a gun, which suddenly startled me because the atmosphere of my hometown made me react particularly sensitively. I thought we couldn't go in, but Fu Dong had already stepped into the temple gate, so I followed him in. I don't want to describe everything inside the temple. I think everyone who has been to Nanjing knows about it.

We walked into the [Tea Room] and sat down next to a table with windows on two sides. When I looked inside, there was still no one there, only heavier rain falling outside the building. After a while, a person carrying a water bottle and a snack box came to make two bowls of tea for us. I craned my neck to look out the window, and Fu Dong pointed out to me where Taicheng was, where Tianbao City was, and where Xuanwu Lake was. So I quietly enjoyed the magnificent scenery of the river and mountains and the quiet, lonely rain. Fu Dong didn't say anything, just drank tea by himself. So I thought of Emperor Wu of Liang, who came from a prominent family and established a kingdom and dominated the world. I thought of him throwing himself into Buddhism, and I thought of him being trapped by Hou Jing. I admired his heroism and pitied his ignorance. I even suspected that heroism and ignorance should be used as linked words. In less than a quarter of an hour, all the historical sites of Jiangnan that I could remember had been replayed in my mind. What were my feelings? I couldn't analyze it myself at the time. I just felt that there was a kind of artistic conception in my heart. This artistic conception didn't seem to be exclusive to the ancients, and it seemed to be very closely related to myself, even to the trivial matter of my reunion with Fu Dong. But I finally couldn't figure out what that would have to do with me.

I turned to look at Fu Dong. He was sitting with his back to the window, his feet propped up on another stool, his eyes seemingly fixed on the three words "Tea Room". He was chewing on a piece of dried beef that I had brought from my hometown. He didn't know I was looking at him. After a while, he suddenly shook his head and softly said,

(Not clever.)

Why did he suddenly utter this three-word exclamation? I suddenly felt strange. Could it be that he said the words were not well written?

(Hey, what are you commenting on?)

(I didn't think about anything.) He shook his head and responded with an irrelevant reply. Suddenly, he suddenly ordered me,

(Look at these couplets, why must they talk about the golden powder of the Six Dynasties? Why must everyone strike up such an antiquated tone of no return? This is our new capital.) He stopped speaking, chewing his beef.

I was idle at the time, so I also read those couplets and looked at the names signed on them. Indeed, there was no vitality in them at this time. All kinds of decorations on the floor were opposite each other, each in a daze. The various meanings in the couplets pressed down on the air on the floor, and it naturally became desolate. Looking into the distance again, the lake, mountains, city walls, and misty rain were tightly locked, making the whole scene a dizzy world. So all the scenic spots and a history of Jiangnan disappeared from my chest. I couldn't even think about where I was now and why he had come here. Suddenly, I thought of my hometown, my world of soldiers and bandits, my educational experience, my life full of holes, etc. I also sighed deeply, (I'm tired of it).

Fu Dong stood up, took a sip of tea, smiled at me and said,

(Actually, Jiming Temple can be given a new meaning. "In the darkness of the storm, the rooster crows endlessly." Shouldn't these two sentences be worth reflecting on for those in the newly built capital? After thinking again and again, although we have also experienced many vicissitudes, actually the days of this life are still very long. If the heart turns to ashes too early, isn't the second half of life even harder? So no matter how difficult life is, you have to cheer yourself up. Although I now often find fun in leisure, leisure often gives me such nostalgia. I always feel that my destined path has not been completed.)

Then he told me very happily about his experiences in the past few years, which were completely different from when he came. I also left the floor and the scenery and listened attentively. We seemed to see the sunlight, see the grassland, see the flowing water, and the strength in our bodies seemed to increase as if it were being injected from a small pipe.

When the clouds cleared and the sun came out, we came out of the temple, walked back through the newly refreshed forest after the rain.

Night Soulless

Oh, it's as if some strange sound is blowing into my head.

Artsybashev's Night

My heart, like someone buried alive in a tomb, is so depressed it wants to jump out of my body.

The electric light is trembling, just like the turmoil of my emotions, trembling in the same way. The symphony of the night market comes from afar, mixed with the sound of the landladies on the floor below playing mahjong, and the shouts of vendors selling late-night snacks outside. Tonight, oh, these sounds are especially grating on my nerves.

Pray, implore the Heavenly Father to grant strength, to rescue a suffering soul from the throes of pain. I look up at the black sky twinkling with stars, but what's the use? All reason has lost its power, let alone a nonexistent god.

I turned off the electric light. I imagined that darkness might bring peace to my soul.

I shout, but my voice scatters in the darkness without echoing back.

I become angry, I flee the small room, I flee the small room, I want to hit someone, I want to kill someone, and I even want to set a fire.

Finally, hanging my head, silent as a shadow, I tread on the cobblestone road, but the cobblestone road makes me angry. I want to curse the Chinese municipality. I kick the cobblestone road with my leather shoes. A team of police passes by me. Hush, a row of black dogs. Suddenly, I also realize that kicking the cobblestone road with my leather shoes is a loss for myself.

Standing below a tall building, I shout, looking at the windows above,

(Alas, alas, alas!) The sound bumps around on the wall, but there is no answer. Disheartened, I walk away. I think,

(Alas, perhaps he's hiding in his room, organizing a new work, deliberately not answering those who visit him. Bah, you ghoul, I'll go back and work hard too, and finish writing that "Miss Malan.")

But I don't go back on the way back. My soul is roaring,

(Heart, burst open! The surroundings are so desolate, all sounds seem like the silent cries of a mute, meaningless. Women, I definitely don't need anything to do with women. What do I need? I need an earthquake, or else I need to see the sky falling down, otherwise, I'll suffocate. What to do? My heart wants to jump out, but the walls of flesh and bone imprison it firmly. Burst open, heart,...)

As I walk, I suddenly remember that I should go find my enemy. I want to tell my enemy,

(Listen, I beg you to listen, to all these strange dreams. Come, I'll tell you, you are not my enemy, we are good friends, look at my tears. Please come and kiss me. Enemy, I'll tell you, about news of her, she is already sleeping in the arms of a man with four hundred yuan a month. You must believe that I am not deceiving you. Think, why did I disregard life and death to embark on a long march to the North Country when snow was flying last year? Now I have returned south. I heard that she has divorced you too. So I wanted to write you a long letter several times, although this long letter was never written several times, for fear of making people cry, perhaps for fear of making you laugh. Ah, enemy, listen, I've come to vomit everything to you, all these strange dreams,...)

I made up my mind, pushed open his door, and dragged my trembling legs up the stairs.

(You haven't moved?) I say this to him after a long time. Two friends were also sitting in his room. (Yes, I haven't moved. Is there something you need?)

(No, yes, I'm leaving.) I suddenly felt insulted and fled his room. He was still asking, (Is there something you need?)

With a burning face, I left the dark alleyway and entered the noisy street center. The peach-colored shadows of women flutter past, carrying the fragrance of powder, immediately conjuring up thoughts of sexual desire in the minds of young men. The noise of the RADIO at the entrance of a shop is playing a Shanghai dialect ditty, making one's nerves tingle,...)

I stood in front of the GOOSE CAFE, watching a dancing girl with swaying hips go up the stone steps. I wanted to follow her inside. I hesitated, but in the end, I just left there.

I don't need to see women, these, animals with white bodies, things with clever mouths and flowing eyes, goblins with swaying hips,...

I walked away in a huff, depression and vexation still entrenched in my heart.

From the bustling city, I walked into a quiet street. Carrying my disappointment, I trudged back towards my room. By the dark roadside, there were starving beggars moaning. I grabbed a handful of copper coins from my pocket and scattered them to them, but then I regretted it. I felt that this kind of humanitarianism, this act of compassion, was ridiculous.

I returned to the small room again, and turned on the light.

I slumped down at the table cluttered with paper and books, suddenly feeling sadness in my heart.

The night wind cooled my cheeks,

I felt the warmth of tears,

My soul was hypnotized...

Jingwu Association's New Year Trip

Location: Changshu

The travel group of the North Sichuan Road Jingwu Athletic Association, considering that Changshu is an area where famous Jiangnan scenic spots gather, with beautiful scenery and outstanding people, not inferior to Hangzhou's West Lake, is now taking advantage of the National Calendar New Year holiday to travel to the area. Return to Shanghai from Yu via the original route. Famous gardens include Huyin, Zhao Garden, Zhi Garden, Park, and Yan Garden. The fee for members is eight yuan and a half per person, including transportation, accommodation, and meals. An Outline of Journalistic Literature by Tang Zenghongyang

Written by Huang Tianpeng

In the past year or two, most of the domestic journalists have paid attention to the practical research of new literature, because in the modern era where journalism is gradually becoming prosperous, if you only rely on past experience in serving the newspaper industry, and the knowledge of journalism that you have obtained sporadically, of course, it is still impossible to use it freely. At least, in terms of theory, you feel lack and bitterness. Therefore, well-known foreign professionals in journalism, in addition to having extremely rich experience in this industry, also have in-depth research on journalism. Because of this, foreign countries pay attention to the reality of the journalism industry after our country, but their rate of development has far exceeded our country. This amazing progress is clear to anyone who pays attention to the journalism industry. Generally speaking, it is because they attach equal importance to practice and research that they have evolved into today's perfect achievements. Moreover, most of the people engaged in journalism in foreign countries have already built a considerable foundation in literature, or it can be said that they are journalism experts and writers. This is a very obvious fact, and I don't need to give examples. In the Chinese journalism industry, there has recently been a gratifying and praiseworthy phenomenon, that is, those engaged in journalism, in addition to using the knowledge they have gained from experience, pay attention to specialized research in journalism, which is of great relevance to the future of the Chinese journalism industry, and at least can promote the progress of journalism and have a new expression. If we continue to work hard in this way academically, perhaps China's journalism industry can keep pace with foreign countries in the near future, which is also an inevitable phenomenon. What makes us particularly happy is that scholars who have specialized in journalism are willing to contribute the insights of this research to the world, which is indeed worthy of our praise. Regarding this, Mr. Huang Tianpeng can be said to be one of the most hardworking and contributing. We only need to see that among the recent massive publications on journalism theory in the market, the most abundant one is undoubtedly Mr. Huang's. This book (An Outline of Journalistic Literature) can be regarded as the most valuable one. We should pay deep attention to it.

Because most of the books on journalism published on the market belong to newspaper editing methods, newspaper interviewing methods, how to become a journalist, and newspaper research, etc. This is also the case in foreign newspapers, but Huang's is the first to discuss journalistic literature. This point alone shows the greatness of the author. Regarding this kind of writing, it is completely based on the thorough research and the best possible expression. There is simply nothing similar to this kind of writing that can be referred to. Those who pay attention to journalism can understand this without any doubt.

The whole book is divided into nine chapters. Each chapter has correct arguments and precise insights. The first chapter (Introduction to Journalistic Literature) talks about the motivation for writing this book, citing the arguments of foreign journalism scholars as the starting point, which is particularly valuable and gratifying. Secondly, it explains the process of the establishment of material science and the relationship between newspapers and history. This point is extremely important in journalistic literature, so the author cites historical facts from ancient and modern China and foreign countries as the basis, in great detail. The necessity of research on journalistic literature is even more vividly expressed. The second chapter (The Establishment of Journalistic Literature) talks about the initial prototype of journalistic literature. Regarding this, the author first argues about the origin of newspapers, and objectively discusses the (China and Foreign News) and (Shiwu Bao) etc., which were published one after another after the war between China and Japan, as well as their article style and the schools of authors. Secondly, it discusses how to create the foundation of journalistic literature, the outline of Chinese literature, and records about journalistic literature. The third chapter (The Characteristics of Journalistic Literature), in order to make it easier for readers to understand, the author divides the characteristics of journalistic literature into three points: (1) timeliness, (2) popularity, (3) interest. Such an analysis is of course very meaningful. At the same time, these three characteristics are further explained, explaining its position and value in literature. The fourth chapter (The Genre of Journalistic Literature) is based on history, which is of course not easy to be wrong. For example, the historical records of the past are (1) Zuo Zhuan style, (2) Historical Records style, (3) Liaozhai style. Secondly, it is the news record, (1) Outline method, (2) Flashback method, (3) Summary method, with detailed explanations. Finally, through comparative research on these three kinds of records, readers can understand their advantages and disadvantages, and the editing methods that should be adopted. The fifth chapter (The Evolution of Journalistic Literature) is described in great detail, and is divided into three sections: (1) The era of political commentary, (2) The era of news, (3) Supplementary edition texts, (4) Conclusion. Especially the third section is mostly the author's unique insights, which can make us feel the same. The sixth chapter (The Changes of Journalistic Literature) first talks about the prediction of the literary revolution, then the process of the revolutionary movement, and finally the various influences of new new literature. This chapter is indeed extremely important, even in history, the changes in journalistic literature also occupy an important position. The seventh chapter (The Classification of Journalistic Literature), the first section is an introduction, (A) the approximate categories of texts on newspapers, (B) the unique characteristics of each, (C) the common principles of literature and art, the second section is commentary, (A) the meaning of commentary, (B) providing problems and annotating news, (C) the classification of commentary, (D) the three major schools in the commentary world recently, (E) the conditions for commentators, the third section is news, (1) telegrams, (A) notes on telegrams, (B) the secret of conciseness, (C) the procedures for compiling telegrams, (D) examples of choosing between special telegrams and foreign telegrams, (2) interviews, (A) the principles and schools of ordinary interview production, (B) the key points of news description techniques, (C) eight methods and examples in two categories of time and space, (3) communications, (A) the connotation and external form of special communications, (B) systematic narration, (C) interesting description, (D) impression notes, (4) headlines, (A) the art of news headlines, (B) revealing the outline and attracting attention, (C) four principles to abide by and four prohibitions, (D) examples of formats, (E) the recent progress view, the fourth section is recreational literature, (A) the two major trends of recreational literature, (B) the enjoyment of modern material life, (C) the appreciation of human spiritual life, the fifth section is advertising literature, (A) the news value of advertising, (B) nature, (C) structure, (D) style, (E) title, (F) various studies, (G) news literature of advertising. This chapter occupies the most space in the whole book, and the excerpts in the sections are extremely detailed, most of which are sufficient for us to refer to. The eighth chapter (The Power of Journalistic Literature), regarding this chapter, the author divides it into four characteristics: (1) universality, (2) continuity, (3) speed, (4) abundance, and the metaphor of human footprints. This kind of discussion should have objective value, because without explaining this kind of power, readers will definitely not be able to understand the unique position of journalistic literature, etc. The ninth chapter (The Future of Journalistic Literature), (1) the popularization of journalistic literature, (2) journalistic literature as the literature of the masses, (3) the discussion of the problem of classical Chinese and vernacular Chinese in newspaper articles, (4) the new trend of Mandarinization. This chapter is really very important in today's journalistic literature. Although the author has hopes for the future, it is also a major problem that needs to be solved most urgently at present. However, the author has explained it in detail and thoroughly here.

In short, after reading Mr. Huang's masterpiece, we can

understand the essential theoretical foundation of journalistic literature. At the same time, the power of newspapers is expanding day by day, so we really need to focus on the study of journalism, and how to improve the domestic newspapers and how to organize them precisely are all matters that must be discussed in detail at present. This book (Journalistic Literature) shows the author's unique insights everywhere, which is obviously the result of his research. We cannot help but say that it is a very valuable book on domestic journalism monographs. We hope that those who study journalism and those who love journalism will pay deep attention to it.
